< review>
First class modern equipment and technics provided.  I needed a crown and they scanned my teeth and had a 3D printed crown made.  While waiting for the crown to come in my temporary crown came loose.  It is very rare to have one come loose; however the office responded to my message within a few hours and arranged to have a employee meet me at the office.  This was on a Sunday on Memorial day weekend.  This is a testament  to their dedication to their patients.  The lady who showed up was apologetic about my situation and was friendly and professional even with the fact she had to come in on a holiday weekend.  She quickly made some adjustments to my temporary crown and securely placed it back on the tooth.  This is truly  a dental office that puts their patients needs first.< /review>

<user_id>105117703295156699597</user_id><Name>Troy N<//Name><time>1522007997629</time><Rate>4</Rate>< Review>
A nice place for a nerf gun battle. A nice size for larger parties but the obstacles in their play area is a bit sparse. You have 75 minutes of play which has a good amount of time but it's mostly free play. There was one game between teams with scoring and that was really fun. A bit more "organized" play would have been nice but the kids didn't seem to mind.

Although you can upgrade the party for $4/child so they can try out a larger variety of guns I would recommend you stay basic. The larger guns tend to jam more and take longer to load.

You can bring in water and a fruit plate platter but food and drinks for a party needs to be ordered thru the venue.</Review>

<Text>Sugared and Lashed Studio is Claremont's *newest* hidden gem for wellness & beauty. Unlike many small locally owned businesses, the prices are VERY reasonable and the owner, Danielle, is almost always on-site. Additionally, the environment is very welcoming, there are always complimentary fresh organic teas, juices, infusions, cookies, etc. waiting for you when you arrive, and the products used don't contain many of the harsh chemicals used at other studios. The treatments I receive here completely changed my lifestyle and the way I look at myself. I will definitely continue booking treatments at Sugared and Lashed Studio.

Being a natural blonde, I also have the joy of light brown & blonde brows, and lashes with blonde bases and tips... *sigh*... This doesn't exactly make for a stunning bold brow & lush lash effect. Moreover, I don't like wearing a lot of makeup because I have extremely sensitive skin. However, when owner, Danielle, recommended I try a keratin lash lift paired with the henna brow and lash tints, it was a total game changer!

Danielle has been working with my brows, allowing them to grow out fuller than what was typical for me in the past, then with the henna tint she can incorporate all my "little blondies" (which used to just be wishful thinking, but ultimately nuisances) into the natural brow. Once the whole brow is the warm shade of brown I like, Danielle uses hard wax to gently clean and shape them for a full, but polished look. The result? Fuller/thicker brows than I ever thought possible! Plus, without all the extra synthetics and chemicals, I never experience any irritation after treatment. (See henna brow and lash tints + brow hard wax before & after photos below)

While I follow up on my lash henna tinting maintenance just as often as my brow henna tinting (about once every two to four weeks as needed), I *do* have to wait longer in between keratin lash lifts. The lash henna tint Danielle uses for me comes out as the jet black color I look for when I used to wear the occasional mascara. I love how much length is "added" to my lashes just from the henna alone, but when paired with the keratin lash lift (last one done before these photos was 3 months ago) it looks like I'm *wearing* lashes even though they're all mine and all natural. < Text>
I find it funny how passionate the reviews are on this building. Besides the museum on the first floor it is just an administrative hub for the international outreach programs for the Church and has just has various office spaces, conference rooms, files, etc. so wouldn't be of general interest.

If you want to see what they do, just go to the 8 story information center they put just a few blocks down on the corner of Hollywood and Mccadden. (As a trivia fact that is the same corner where the first LGBT Pride parade was held in LA over 40 years ago!).

You can also go to the next street over on Franklin, or the the next street over in the opposite direction on Sunset Blvd, or a little further down on Hillhurst or just over the hill in Burbank.

Scientology owns more real estate in Hollywood than anyone else for the last 30 years or so, and wont be leaving anytime soon, so you have plenty of chances and locations to explore if you are interested.

If you don't want to leave the house you can tune in anytime to their just- launched TV network broadcasting from Hollywood to Direct TV Channel 320, all online streaming platforms including Apple TV or on the Scientology Network App for Android and I-phone.< /Text>

The man was really a polymath (person of wide-ranging knowledge or learning), probably with a wider range than Leonardo Da Vinci, and he lived a very active life‚Äîvery interesting tour; unlike any other.

There are a lot of malicious people in media ready to denigrate ANY religion as long as they can "get away with it."  Don't listen to propaganda; go visit and talk to some actual Scientologists and make up your own mind.

By the way, I just looked at there are several hundred fake one-star reviews from six years ago that are pretty obviously all from the same disgruntled person using a bunch of fake accounts (they all are from "A Google User" and most are completely non-sequitur or empty). < review>
I've been to a few to check it out. I'm a very bright individual myself, so there is nothing actually useful that any church or organization can teach me that I already haven't learned on my own. All my lessons from life and experience itself. I agree Scientology's presentation is silly and feels fictional which makes it hard to take them seriously, but they do make valid points if you understand what they try to explain, but fail to present it to others who aren't already part of their groups. I can see the founder had good intentions, but now passed away. Who ever is now running the show seems to be using this more as a mean to gather money than to focus on the individuals, hence why it feels like a bunch of cheesy advertisement about their books, with fiction novel covers. They are like any other religion and church I've come across: "Support us, buy books from us, donate what you don't need, so we can give it to the needy and take credit for it that we did something, but never really waste any money and rarely out our way to truly help someone." That seems to be many church and religions' golden rule. I don't have a problem with Scientology other than them following that same rule. Their teachings are in ways accurate and sincere but misrepresented and feel like bullshit, due to poor management and communication. I would however deem anyone as mentally confused or lost, that attacks this belief system but believe in an inaccurate, heavily edited and mistranslated 2000 year old book about a man who believed himself to be god and freed the men in this world of their sin but left the world to continue in conflict. Scientology is silly, but doesn't go out their way to push bullshit down your throat or completely misguide already lost individuals, like other religions do, unless you walk into their buildings, but still more tolerable I'd say. I put good in quality, but I actually consider my experience and their quality as Fair.

ONE IMPORTANT NOTE TO REVIEWERS:

The founder is dead, do not blame him for your bad experiences. Judging one's beliefs due to being Sci Fi writers is as low as you can go. I am a Sci Fi writer myself, and I implement many of my beliefs and feelings to my stories, just as many writers, artist, and cultures do to their forms of arts. Just as fiction was implemented to many religions, the bible, and is even incorporated with science to prove what may be possible. Sometimes implementing beliefs, knowledge and advice in entertainment is the only way to pass it on to those with short attention spans or lacking interest in raw information. Lets agree that we all need to learn respect, and reflection, to understand one another better in life. - Avenx<//review>

< Text>
This place has changed ownership so some of the past reviews might not be so good. But the new owner has turned Wes's back around to what it was years ago. I love this little feed store. I  go  when I need things like hay or Timothy Hay or some feed for wild birds or chickens. On this trip I went for hay dor my manger scene. I was able to buy part of a bale, (one bale would have been $8, not a lot of money but I didn't need a whole bale of hay) While I was there I noticed he didn't have any chickens for sale. The owner told me that a disease has hit the southern California area, Virulent Newcastle Disease (VND) (it is deadly to birds especially chickens and is very contagious) so he can't sell chicks until December. Great service, friendly people, small and interesting. It's local kind of business that I really love.<//Text>

< Review>
Hand down, BEST Sandwiches in San Francisco! I'm so lucky to live in the Excelsior and have Roxie's just a hop, skip and jump away! My go to is a Regular Mortadella on Sourdough, everything on it, toasted. Some people think the bread to meat ratio is 60:40 but I think it's perfect. The guys that run the place are hilarious and never fail to make everyone feel welcome.

Although getting in line can be a bit confusing for people when they first come here, it's totally worth it. (For those who haven't tried Roxie's yet: When you come in the front door, walk along the drinks and sodas, and the line starts at the first deli case)

Keep up the great work, Roxie's</Review>
